data-v-163e157e><a href="/w/%EA%B4%80%EA%B3%84" data-v-163e157e><!---->관계</a> <!----></h1> <div class="enGXrajm" data-v-163e157e>최근 수정 시각: <time datetime="2023-09-24T08:25:10.000Z" data-v-163e157e>2023-09-24 08:25:10</time></div> <!----> <div data-v-163e157e></div><div data-v-163e157e></div><div data-v-163e157e></div><div data-v-163e157e></div> <div data-v-163e157e data-v-163e157e data-v-163e157e><div data-v-163e157e data-v-163e157e><div data-v-163e157e data-v-163e157e><div data-v-683a701b data-v-163e157e><!----> <!----> <!----> <div class="4b667763" data-v-683a701b data-v-683a701b><div data-v-60a9fc16 data-v-683a701b><div class="JRul4hqE" data-v-60a9fc16></div> <ul data-v-60a9fc16><li data-v-60a9fc16><a href="/w/%EB%B6%84%EB%A5%98:%EC%A7%91%ED%95%A9%EB%A1%A0" data-v-60a9fc16>집합론</a></li><li data-v-60a9fc16><a href="/w/%EB%B6%84%EB%A5%98:%EB%85%BC%EB%A6%AC%ED%95%99" data-v-60a9fc16>논리학</a></li><li data-v-60a9fc16><a href="/w/%EB%B6%84%EB%A5%98:%ED%95%9C%EC%9E%90%EC%96%B4" data-v-60a9fc16>한자어</a></li></ul></div></div> <!----> <div class="4b667763" data-v-683a701b></div><div class="4b667763" data-v-683a701b></div><div class="4b667763" data-v-683a701b></div><div class="4b667763" data-v-683a701b></div><div class="4b667763" data-v-683a701b></div><div class="4b667763" data-v-683a701b></div><div class="4b667763" data-v-683a701b></div> <div data-v-683a701b></div><div data-v-683a701b></div><div data-v-683a701b></div><div data-v-683a701b></div><div data-v-683a701b></div><div data-v-683a701b></div> <!----> <div class="4b667763" data-v-683a701b data-v-683a701b><!----> <!----> <div data-v-df92d3b4 data-v-683a701b><div class="_1+UTAYHc" data-v-df92d3b4><div data-v-00420f0c="" class="wiki-paragraph" data-v-df92d3b4><div class='wiki-macro-toc' id='toc' data-v-00420f0c><div class='toc-indent' data-v-00420f0c><span class='toc-item' data-v-00420f0c><a href='#s-1' data-v-00420f0c>1</a>. 개요</span><span class='toc-item' data-v-00420f0c><a href='#s-2' data-v-00420f0c>2</a>. 상세</span><span class='toc-item' data-v-00420f0c><a href='#s-3' data-v-00420f0c>3</a>. <a class='wiki-link-internal' href='/w/%EC%A7%91%ED%95%A9%EB%A1%A0' title='집합론' data-v-00420f0c>집합론</a>에서의 정의</span><div class='toc-indent' data-v-00420f0c><span class='toc-item' data-v-00420f0c><a href='#s-3.1' data-v-00420f0c>3.1</a>. 이항 관계</span><div class='toc-indent' data-v-00420f0c><span class='toc-item' data-v-00420f0c><a href='#s-3.1.1' data-v-00420f0c>3.1.1</a>. 이항 관계의 대표적인 특성들</span></div><span class='toc-item' data-v-00420f0c><a href='#s-3.2' data-v-00420f0c>3.2</a>. 예시</span></div><span class='toc-item' data-v-00420f0c><a href='#s-4' data-v-00420f0c>4</a>. 순서론</span><span class='toc-item' data-v-00420f0c><a href='#s-5' data-v-00420f0c>5</a>. 기타</span></div></div></div><h2 data-v-00420f0c="" class="wiki-heading" data-v-df92d3b4><a id='s-1' href='#toc' data-v-00420f0c>1.</a> <span id='개요' data-v-00420f0c>개요<span class='wiki-edit-section' data-v-00420f0c><a href='/edit/%EA%B4%80%EA%B3%84?section=1' rel='nofollow' data-v-00420f0c>&#91;편집&#93;</a></span></span></h2><div data-v-00420f0c="" class="wiki-heading-content" data-v-df92d3b4><div class='wiki-paragraph' data-v-00420f0c><span class='wiki-size-up-2' data-v-00420f0c><a class='wiki-link-internal' href='/w/%E9%97%9C' title='關' data-v-00420f0c>關</a><a class='wiki-link-internal' href='/w/%E4%BF%82' title='係' data-v-00420f0c>係</a> / Relation</span><br data-v-00420f0c><br data-v-00420f0c>복수의 대상이 서로 관련하여 이루는 특성. <a class='wiki-link-internal' href='/w/%ED%98%84%EB%8C%80' title='현대' data-v-00420f0c>현대</a> <a class='wiki-link-internal' href='/w/%ED%95%9C%EA%B5%AD%EC%96%B4' title='한국어' data-v-00420f0c>한국어</a>에서는 &quot;a, b, c가 관계를 <strong data-v-00420f0c>맺는다</strong> 같은 표현을 주로 쓴다. 예를 들어 &#39;1+1은 2와 <strong data-v-00420f0c>같다</strong>&#39;, &#39;5는 3보다 <strong data-v-00420f0c>크다</strong>&#39;, &#39;철수가 영희에게 사과를 <strong data-v-00420f0c>준다</strong>&#39; 등이 관계를 나타내는 대표적인 예시다.</div></div><h2 data-v-00420f0c="" class="wiki-heading" data-v-df92d3b4><a id='s-2' href='#toc' data-v-00420f0c>2.</a> <span id='상세' data-v-00420f0c>상세<span class='wiki-edit-section' data-v-00420f0c><a href='/edit/%EA%B4%80%EA%B3%84?section=2' rel='nofollow' data-v-00420f0c>&#91;편집&#93;</a></span></span></h2><div data-v-00420f0c="" class="wiki-heading-content" data-v-df92d3b4><div class='wiki-paragraph' data-v-00420f0c>세상에는 매우 다양한 관계들이 있다. 나무위키에서 다루는 대표적인 관계들은 <a class='wiki-link-internal' href='/w/%EB%8C%80%EA%B5%AD%EA%B4%80%EA%B3%84%EC%9D%BC%EB%9E%8C' title='대국관계일람' data-v-00420f0c>대국관계일람</a>, <a class='wiki-link-internal' href='/w/%EA%B0%80%EC%A1%B1%EA%B4%80%EA%B3%84' title='가족관계' data-v-00420f0c>가족관계</a> 같은 문서들에서 확인할 수 있다.<br data-v-00420f0c><br data-v-00420f0c>위 예시들에서 나타나듯 자연 <a class='wiki-link-internal' href='/w/%EC%96%B8%EC%96%B4' title='언어' data-v-00420f0c>언어</a>에서 관계는 <a class='wiki-link-internal' href='/w/%EB%8F%99%EC%82%AC(%ED%92%88%EC%82%AC)' title='동사(품사)' data-v-00420f0c>동사</a>, <a class='wiki-link-internal' href='/w/%ED%98%95%EC%9A%A9%EC%82%AC' title='형용사' data-v-00420f0c>형용사</a>처럼 <a class='wiki-link-internal' href='/w/%EC%88%A0%EC%96%B4' title='술어' data-v-00420f0c>술어</a> 역할을 하는 어휘에 의해 표현된다. 따라서 <a class='wiki-link-internal' href='/w/%EC%88%98%EB%A6%AC%EB%85%BC%EB%A6%AC%ED%95%99' title='수리논리학' data-v-00420f0c>수리논리학</a>에서 관계는 논항이 여럿인 술어, 즉 다항 술어(polyadic predicate)로 나타낸다. 1항 술어가 나타내는 것이 <a class='wiki-link-internal' href='/w/%EC%86%8D%EC%84%B1' title='속성' data-v-00420f0c>속성</a>이라고 여겨지므로, <a class='wiki-link-internal' href='/w/%ED%98%95%EC%9D%B4%EC%83%81%ED%95%99' title='형이상학' data-v-00420f0c>형이상학</a>에서는 다항 술어가 나타내는 것인 관계가 속성과 매우 유사한 것 혹은 속성의 일종이라고 분석하는 경우가 일반적이다. 후자인 경우 관계는 1항 속성(monadic property)에 대비하여 &quot;다항 속성&quot;, 혹은 &quot;관계적 속성(relational property)&quot;라고 부르고는 한다.<br data-v-00420f0c><br data-v-00420f0c><a class='wiki-link-internal' href='/w/%EA%B3%A0%ED%8B%80%EB%A1%9C%ED%94%84%20%ED%94%84%EB%A0%88%EA%B2%8C' title='고틀로프 프레게' data-v-00420f0c>고틀로프 프레게</a>가 관계를 <a class='wiki-link-internal' href='/w/%ED%95%A8%EC%88%98' title='함수' data-v-00420f0c>함수</a>로 분석한 이래로 관계는 대개 <a class='wiki-link-internal' href='/w/%EC%A7%91%ED%95%A9%EB%A1%A0' title='집합론' data-v-00420f0c>집합론</a>을 통해 분석된다. 자세한 내용은 <a class='wiki-link-internal' href='#s-2' title='' data-v-00420f0c>하단 문서로</a>. 다만 엄밀히 따지자면 <a class='wiki-link-internal' href='/w/%EC%88%98%EB%A6%AC%EB%85%BC%EB%A6%AC%ED%95%99' title='수리논리학' data-v-00420f0c>수리논리학</a>적 관점에서 하단 정의는 관계의 외연(extension)에 대한 정의로 이해된다. 예를 들어 <a class='wiki-link-internal' href='/w/ZFC%20%EA%B3%B5%EB%A6%AC%EA%B3%84' title='ZFC 공리계' data-v-00420f0c>표준적 집합론</a>의 언어에서 이항 술어인 &quot;∈&quot;이 표현하는 관계, 즉 원소-집합 관계는 기초적인 것으로 전제되어야만 하기 때문이다.<br data-v-00420f0c></div></div><h2 data-v-00420f0c="" class="wiki-heading" data-v-df92d3b4><a id='s-3' href='#toc' data-v-00420f0c>3.</a> <span id='집합론에서의 정의' data-v-00420f0c><a class='wiki-link-internal' href='/w/%EC%A7%91%ED%95%A9%EB%A1%A0' title='집합론' data-v-00420f0c>집합론</a>에서의 정의<span class='wiki-edit-section' data-v-00420f0c><a href='/edit/%EA%B4%80%EA%B3%84?section=3' rel='nofollow' data-v-00420f0c>&#91;편집&#93;</a></span></span></h2><div data-v-00420f0c="" class="wiki-heading-content" data-v-df92d3b4><div 한쪽 끝이 막혀 있는 화살표(<span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo>↦</mo></mrow><annotation data-v-df92d3b4><a id='s-3.1' href='#toc' data-v-00420f0c>3.1.</a> <span id='이항 관계' data-v-00420f0c>이항 관계<span class='wiki-edit-section' data-v-00420f0c><a href='/edit/%EA%B4%80%EA%B3%84?section=4' rel='nofollow' data-v-00420f0c>&#91;편집&#93;</a></span></span></h3><div data-v-00420f0c="" class="wiki-heading-content" data-v-df92d3b4><div class='wiki-paragraph' data-v-00420f0c><strong data-v-00420f0c>이항 관계(Binary Relation, 二項關係)</strong>란 위 정의를 따르되 다만 <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>n</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>2</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">n=2</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.43056em;vertical-align:0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">n</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.64444em;vertical-align:0em;"></span><span class="mord">2</span></span></span></span>인 경우에 해당한다. 즉 집합 <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>X</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>Y</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">X, Y</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8777699999999999em;vertical-align:-0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.16666666666666666em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.22222em;">Y</span></span></span></span>와 사이의 이항 관계 <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>R</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">R</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.68333em;vertical-align:0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.00773em;">R</span></span></span></span>는 곱집합 <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>X</mi><mo>×</mo><mi>Y</mi><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo fence="true">{</mo><mrow><mo fence="true">(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>y</mi><mo fence="true">)</mo></mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">∣</mi><mi>x</mi><mo>∈</mo><mi>X</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>y</mi><mo>∈</mo><mi>Y</mi><mo fence="true">}</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">X\times Y=\left\{\left(x, y\right)|x\in X, y\in Y\right\}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.76666em;vertical-align:-0.08333em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222222222222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">×</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222222222222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.68333em;vertical-align:0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.22222em;">Y</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="minner"><span class="mopen delimcenter" style="top:0em;">{</span><span class="minner"><span class="mopen delimcenter" style="top:0em;">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.16666666666666666em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.03588em;">y</span><span class="mclose delimcenter" style="top:0em;">)</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.16666666666666666em;"></span><span class="mord">∣</span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span><span class="mrel">∈</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.16666666666666666em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.03588em;">y</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span><span class="mrel">∈</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.22222em;">Y</span><span class="mclose delimcenter" style="top:0em;">}</span></span></span></span></span>의 부분집합 <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>G</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">G</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.68333em;vertical-align:0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">G</span></span></span></span>에 대해 순서 3중체 <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo fence="true">(</mo><mi>X</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>Y</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>G</mi><mo fence="true">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\left(X, Y, G\right)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="minner"><span class="mopen delimcenter" style="top:0em;">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.16666666666666666em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" delimcenter" style="top:0em;">)</span></span></span></span></span>로 정의되거나, 혹은 <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>G</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">G</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.68333em;vertical-align:0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">G</span></span></span></span>로 정의된다. 후자의 경우 <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>R</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">R</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.68333em;vertical-align:0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.00773em;">R</span></span></span></span>은 집합 <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>X</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>Y</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">X, Y</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8777699999999999em;vertical-align:-0.19444em;"></span><span style="margin-right:0.22222em;">Y</span></span></span></span> 각각의 원소로 이루어진 순서 2중체, 즉 <a class='wiki-link-internal' href='/w/%EC%88%9C%EC%84%9C%EC%8C%8D' title='순서쌍' data-v-00420f0c>순서쌍</a>들의 집합으로 정의되는 것이다.<br data-v-00420f0c><br data-v-00420f0c>그리고 이항 관계에 한하여 <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>X</mi><mo class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.16666666666666666em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.22222em;">Y</span></span></span></span> 각각의 어떤 원소 <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>y</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">x, y</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.625em;vertical-align:-0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.16666666666666666em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.03588em;">y</span></span></span></span>가 <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mrow><mo fence="true">(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>y</mi><mo fence="true">)</mo></mrow><mo>∈</mo><mi>G</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\left(x, y\right)\in G</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="minner"><span xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>Y</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">Y</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.68333em;vertical-align:0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.22222em;">Y</span></span></span></span> 사이의 이항 관계 <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>R</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">R</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.68333em;vertical-align:0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.00773em;">R</span></span></span></span>이 있고, <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>Y</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">Y</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.68333em;vertical-align:0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.22222em;">Y</span></span></span></span>와 <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>Z</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">Z</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.68333em;vertical-align:0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.07153em;">Z</span></span></span></span> 사이의 이항 관계 <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>S</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">S</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.68333em;vertical-align:0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.05764em;">S</span></span></span></span>가 있다고 할 때, <strong data-v-00420f0c>합성 이항 관계</strong> <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>S</mi><mo>∘</mo><mi>R</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">S\circ R</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.68333em;vertical-align:0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.00773em;">R</span></span></span></span>는 <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>H</mi><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo fence="true">{</mo><mrow><mo fence="true">(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>z</mi><mo fence="true">)</mo></mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">∣</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">∃</mi><mi>y</mi><mo>∈</mo><mi>Y</mi><mo>:</mo><mi>x</mi><mi>R</mi><mi>y</mi><mtext> </mtext><mtext> and</mtext><mtext> </mtext><mtext> </mtext><mi>y</mi><mi>S</mi><mi>z</mi><mo fence="true">}</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">H=\left\{\left(x, z\right)|\exists y \in Y : xRy \,\ \text{and} \,\ ySz\right\}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.68333em;vertical-align:0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" delimcenter" style="top:0em;">}</span></span></span></span></span>에 대하여 순서모음 <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo H\right)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span mathvariant="normal" lspace="0em" rspace="0em">′</mo></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">H&#x27;</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.751892em;vertical-align:0em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" mtight">′</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>로 정의된다.<br data-v-00420f0c><br data-v-00420f0c><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>X</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">X</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" data-v-00420f0c>3.1.1.</a> <span id='이항 관계의 대표적인 특성들' data-v-00420f0c>이항 관계의 대표적인 특성들<span class='wiki-edit-section' data-v-00420f0c><a href='/edit/%EA%B4%80%EA%B3%84?section=5' rel='nofollow' data-v-00420f0c>&#91;편집&#93;</a></span></span></h4><div data-v-00420f0c="" class="wiki-heading-content" data-v-df92d3b4><div class='wiki-paragraph' data-v-00420f0c>집합 <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>X</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">X</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.68333em;vertical-align:0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.07847em;">X</span></span></span></span> 위의 이항 관계 <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>R</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">R</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" style="margin-right:0.00773em;">R</span></span></span></span>이 띨 수 있는 대표적인 성질들은 다음과 같다:</div><ul class='wiki-list' data-v-00420f0c><li data-v-00420f0c><div class='wiki-paragraph' data-v-00420f0c><strong data-v-00420f0c>반사성</strong>(or 재귀성; reflexivity): <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">∀</mi><mi>x</mi><mo>∈</mo><mi>X</mi><mo>:</mo><mi>x</mi><mi>R</mi><mi>x</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\forall x \in X: xRx</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.73354em;vertical-align:-0.0391em;"></span><span class="mord">∀</span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span><span class="mrel">∈</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.68333em;vertical-align:0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.68333em;vertical-align:0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.00773em;">R</span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span></span></span></span></div></li><li data-v-00420f0c><div class='wiki-paragraph' data-v-00420f0c><strong data-v-00420f0c>대칭성</strong>(symmetricity): <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">∀</mi><mi>x</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>y</mi><mo>∈</mo><mi>X</mi><mo>:</mo><mi>x</mi><mi>R</mi><mi>y</mi><mo>→</mo><mi>y</mi><mi>R</mi><mi>x</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\forall x,y \in X: xRy \to yRx</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8888799999999999em;vertical-align:-0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord">∀</span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.16666666666666666em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.03588em;">y</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span><span class="mrel">∈</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.68333em;vertical-align:0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span><span class="mrel">:</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8777699999999999em;vertical-align:-0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.00773em;">R</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.03588em;">y</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span><span class="mrel">→</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8777699999999999em;vertical-align:-0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.03588em;">y</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.00773em;">R</span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span></span></span></span></div></li><li data-v-00420f0c><div class='wiki-paragraph' data-v-00420f0c><strong data-v-00420f0c>비대칭성</strong>(asymmetricity): <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">∀</mi><mi>x</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>y</mi><mo>∈</mo><mi>X</mi><mo>:</mo><mi>x</mi><mi>R</mi><mi>y</mi><mo>→</mo><mi class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8888799999999999em;vertical-align:-0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord">∀</span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.16666666666666666em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.03588em;">y</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span><span class="mrel">∈</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.68333em;vertical-align:0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span><span class="mrel">:</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8777699999999999em;vertical-align:-0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.00773em;">R</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.03588em;">y</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span><span class="mrel">→</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8777699999999999em;vertical-align:-0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord">¬</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.03588em;">y</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.00773em;">R</span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span></span></span></span></div></li><li data-v-00420f0c><div class='wiki-paragraph' data-v-00420f0c><strong data-v-00420f0c>반대칭성</strong>(antisymmetricity):  <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">∀</mi><mi>x</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>y</mi><mo>∈</mo><mi>X</mi><mo>:</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>x</mi><mi>R</mi><mi>y</mi><mo>∧</mo><mi>y</mi><mi>R</mi><mi>x</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>→</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo>=</mo><mi>y</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\forall x,y \in X: (xRy \wedge yRx) \to (x=y)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8888799999999999em;vertical-align:-0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord">∀</span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.16666666666666666em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.03588em;">y</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span><span class="mrel">∈</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.68333em;vertical-align:0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span><span class="mrel">:</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.00773em;">R</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.03588em;">y</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222222222222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">∧</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222222222222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.03588em;">y</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.00773em;">R</span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span><span class="mrel">→</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.03588em;">y</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></div></li><li data-v-00420f0c><div class='wiki-paragraph' data-v-00420f0c><strong data-v-00420f0c>전이성</strong>(추이성, 이행성, transitivity): <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">∀</mi><mi>x</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>y</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>z</mi><mo>∈</mo><mi>X</mi><mo>:</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>x</mi><mi>R</mi><mi>y</mi><mo>∧</mo><mi>y</mi><mi>R</mi><mi>z</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>→</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>x</mi><mi>R</mi><mi>z</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\forall x,y,z \in X: (xRy \wedge yRz) \to (xRz)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8888799999999999em;vertical-align:-0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord">∀</span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.16666666666666666em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.03588em;">y</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.16666666666666666em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.04398em;">z</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span><span class="mrel">∈</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.68333em;vertical-align:0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span><span class="mrel">:</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.00773em;">R</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.03588em;">y</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222222222222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">∧</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222222222222222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.03588em;">y</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.00773em;">R</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.04398em;">z</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span><span class="mrel">→</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.00773em;">R</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.04398em;">z</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></div></li><li data-v-00420f0c><div class='wiki-paragraph' data-v-00420f0c><strong data-v-00420f0c><a class='wiki-link-internal' href='/w/%EB%8F%99%EC%B9%98%EA%B4%80%EA%B3%84' title='동치관계' data-v-00420f0c>동치관계</a></strong>: <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>R</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">R</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.68333em;vertical-align:0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.00773em;">R</span></span></span></span>이 반사성, 대칭성, 전이성을 모두 만족시키는 경우.</div></li><li data-v-00420f0c><div class='wiki-paragraph' data-v-00420f0c><strong data-v-00420f0c><a class='wiki-link-internal' href='/w/%EC%88%9C%EC%84%9C%20%EA%B4%80%EA%B3%84' title='순서 관계' data-v-00420f0c>부분순서관계</a></strong>: <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>R</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">R</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.68333em;vertical-align:0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.00773em;">R</span></span></span></span>이 반사성, 반대칭성, 전이성을 모두 만족시키는 경우.<a class='wiki-fn-content' title='순부분순서는 반사성 대신 비반사성을 만족시킨다.' href='#fn-1' data-v-00420f0c><span id='rfn-1' data-v-00420f0c></span>&#91;1&#93;</a></div></li></ul><div class='wiki-paragraph' data-v-00420f0c></div></div><h3 data-v-00420f0c="" class="wiki-heading" data-v-df92d3b4><a id='s-3.2' href='#toc' data-v-00420f0c>3.2.</a> <span id='예시' data-v-00420f0c>예시<span class='wiki-edit-section' data-v-00420f0c><a href='/edit/%EA%B4%80%EA%B3%84?section=6' rel='nofollow' data-v-00420f0c>&#91;편집&#93;</a></span></span></h3><div data-v-00420f0c="" class="wiki-heading-content" data-v-df92d3b4><ul class='wiki-list' data-v-00420f0c><li data-v-00420f0c><div class='wiki-paragraph' data-v-00420f0c><a class='wiki-link-internal' href='/w/%ED%95%A8%EC%88%98' title='함수' data-v-00420f0c>함수</a>는 대표적인 이항 관계의 예이다. 함수 <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>f</mi><mo>:</mo><mi>X</mi><mo>↦</mo><mi>Y</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">f:X\mapsto Y</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8888799999999999em;vertical-align:-0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.10764em;">f</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span><span class="mrel">:</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.69433em;vertical-align:-0.011em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span><span class="mrel">↦</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.68333em;vertical-align:0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.22222em;">Y</span></span></span></span>는 정의역이 <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>X</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">X</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.68333em;vertical-align:0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.07847em;">X</span></span></span></span>이고 정의역의 임의의 원소 <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>x</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">x</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.43056em;vertical-align:0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span></span></span></span>에 대하여 <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>x</mi><mi>R</mi><mi>y</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">xRy</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8777699999999999em;vertical-align:-0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.00773em;">R</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.03588em;">y</span></span></span></span>가 성립하는 <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>y</mi><mo>∈</mo><mi>Y</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">y\in Y</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.7335400000000001em;vertical-align:-0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.03588em;">y</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span><span class="mrel">∈</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.68333em;vertical-align:0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.22222em;">Y</span></span></span></span>가 <a class='wiki-link-internal' href='/w/%EC%9C%A0%EC%9D%BC%EC%84%B1' title='유일성' data-v-00420f0c>유일하게 존재</a>하는 <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>X</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>Y</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">X, Y</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8777699999999999em;vertical-align:-0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.07847em;">X</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.16666666666666666em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.22222em;">Y</span></span></span></span>사이의 이항 관계 <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>R</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">R</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.68333em;vertical-align:0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.00773em;">R</span></span></span></span>와 같다.</div></li></ul><div class='wiki-paragraph' data-v-00420f0c></div></div><h2 data-v-00420f0c="" class="wiki-heading" data-v-df92d3b4><a id='s-4' href='#toc' data-v-00420f0c>4.</a> <span id='순서론' data-v-00420f0c>순서론<span class='wiki-edit-section' data-v-00420f0c><a href='/edit/%EA%B4%80%EA%B3%84?section=7' rel='nofollow' data-v-00420f0c>&#91;편집&#93;</a></span></span></h2><div data-v-00420f0c="" class="wiki-heading-content" data-v-df92d3b4><div class='wiki-paragraph' data-v-00420f0c>순서론(order theory)에서 <a class='wiki-link-internal' href='/w/%EC%88%9C%EC%84%9C%EA%B4%80%EA%B3%84' title='순서관계' data-v-00420f0c>순서관계</a>의 비교 가능성(comparability)은 이항관계의 주요한 하나로 <a class='wiki-link-internal' href='/w/%EC%88%9C%EC%97%B4' title='순열' data-v-00420f0c>순열</a>(permutation 또는 porting)과 <a class='wiki-link-internal' href='/w/%EC%A0%95%EB%A0%AC' title='정렬' data-v-00420f0c>정렬</a>(monotonic order 또는 sorting)을 가능하게 한다. </div><ul class='wiki-list' data-v-00420f0c><li data-v-00420f0c><div class='wiki-paragraph' data-v-00420f0c>비교 가능성(comparability)<br data-v-00420f0c>부분순서집합 <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo fence="true">(</mo><mi>A</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mo>≤</mo><mo fence="true">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\left(A, \leq \right)</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="minner"><span class="mopen delimcenter" style="top:0em;">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span><span class="mrel">≤</span><span class="mclose delimcenter" style="top:0em;">)</span></span></span></span></span>가 주어졌을 때, 집합 <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>A</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">A</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.68333em;vertical-align:0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">A</span></span></span></span>의 두 원소 <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>b</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a, b</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.8888799999999999em;vertical-align:-0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">a</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.16666666666666666em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">b</span></span></span></span>가 <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>a</mi><mo>≤</mo><mi>b</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">a \leq b</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.7719400000000001em;vertical-align:-0.13597em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">a</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span><span class="mrel">≤</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.69444em;vertical-align:0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">b</span></span></span></span>이거나 <span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>b</mi><mo>≤</mo><mi>a</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">b \leq a</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.83041em;vertical-align:-0.13597em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">b</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span><span class="mrel">≤</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.43056em;vertical-align:0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">a</span></span></span></span>이면 a와 b는 <strong data-v-00420f0c>비교 가능하다(comparable)</strong>고 하며, 그렇지 않으면 a와 b는 <strong data-v-00420f0c>비교 불가능하다(incomparable)</strong>고 한다.</div></li></ul><div class='wiki-paragraph' data-v-00420f0c></div></div><h2 data-v-00420f0c="" class="wiki-heading" data-v-df92d3b4><a id='s-5' href='#toc' data-v-00420f0c>5.</a> <span id='기타' data-v-00420f0c>기타<span class='wiki-edit-section' data-v-00420f0c><a href='/edit/%EA%B4%80%EA%B3%84?section=8' rel='nofollow' data-v-00420f0c>&#91;편집&#93;</a></span></span></h2><div data-v-00420f0c="" class="wiki-heading-content" data-v-df92d3b4><ul class='wiki-list' data-v-00420f0c><li data-v-00420f0c><div class='wiki-paragraph' data-v-00420f0c><a class='wiki-link-internal' href='/w/%EC%84%B1%EA%B4%80%EA%B3%84' title='성관계' data-v-00420f0c>성관계</a>를 &#39;관계&#39;라고 표현하는 경우가 있다. 영문의 &#39;intercourse&#39;라는 단어와 대응되며, &#39;sexual&#39;을 제외하고 단독으로 사용할 수 있다. 이 역시 다의어로 &#39;의사소통&#39;의 뜻을 동시에 지니고 있다.</div></li></ul><div class='wiki-paragraph' data-v-00420f0c><br data-v-00420f0c></div></div><div data-v-00420f0c="" class="wiki-macro-footnote" data-v-df92d3b4><span class='footnote-list' data-v-00420f0c><span id='fn-1' data-v-00420f0c></span><a href='#rfn-1' data-v-00420f0c>&#91;1&#93;</a> 순부분순서는 반사성 대신 비반사성을 만족시킨다.</span></div></div> <!----></div> <div data-v-683a701b></div> </div> <!----> <!----></div></div></div></div></div> <div data-v-163e157e></div><div data-v-163e157e></div><div 관계가 속성과 매우 유사한 것 혹은 속성의 일종이라고 분석하는 경우가 일반적이다. 후자인 경우 관계는 1항 속성(monadic property)에 대비하여 &quot;다항 속성&quot;, 혹은 &quot;관계적 속성(relational property)&quot;라고 부르고는 한다.\u003Cbr data-v-00420f0c\u003E\u003Cbr
